    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.framework.util.get_movement_key_data

    local t = {
    	a = { Enum.KeyCode.A, Enum.KeyCode.Left },
    	d = { Enum.KeyCode.D, Enum.KeyCode.Right },
    	jump = { Enum.KeyCode.Space },
    	s = { Enum.KeyCode.S, Enum.KeyCode.Down },
    	w = { Enum.KeyCode.W, Enum.KeyCode.Up }
    }
    return {
    	default = function(p1, p2) --[[ get_movement_key_data | Line: 9 | Upvalues: t (copy) ]]
    		for v2, v3 in t.w do
    			if p2[v3] == true then
    			p1.movementY = p1.movementY + 1
    		for v5, v6 in t.s do
    			if p2[v6] == true then
    			p1.movementY = p1.movementY - 1
    		for v8, v9 in t.a do
    			if p2[v9] == true then
    			p1.movementX = p1.movementX + 1
    		for v11, v12 in t.d do
    			if p2[v12] == true then
    				v10 = v12
    			p1.movementX = p1.movementX - 1
    		if p2[Enum.KeyCode.E] then
    			p1.movementZ = p1.movementZ + 1
    		if p2[Enum.KeyCode.F] then
    			p1.movementZ = p1.movementZ - 1
    		for v14, v15 in t.jump do
    			if p2[v15] == true then
    				v13 = v15
    		return v13 ~= nil
    }

  transition_player_movement_with_momentum (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.framework.util.transition_player_movement_with_momentum
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    return {
    	default = function(p1, p2, p3) --[[ transition_player_movement_with_momentum | Line: 2 ]]
    		local last_jump_lookvector = p1.last_jump_lookvector
    		local v1 = math.atan2(last_jump_lookvector.X, last_jump_lookvector.Z)
    		local v2 = p1.last_jump_input.movementX * math.cos(v1) + p1.last_jump_input.movementY * math.sin(v1)
    		local v3 = -p1.last_jump_input.movementX * math.sin(v1) + p1.last_jump_input.movementY * math.cos(v1)
    		local v4 = p2.movementX * math.cos(v1) + p2.movementY * math.sin(v1)
    		local v5 = -p2.movementX * math.sin(v1) + p2.movementY * math.cos(v1)
    		local v7 = Vector3.new(v2, p2.movementY, v3):Lerp(Vector3.new(v4, p2.movementY, v5), p3)
    		p2.non_relative_x = v7.X
    		p2.non_relative_y = v7.Z
    }

    				vec_deviation = Vector2.new()
    			}

    			return {

    			}

    			local v3 = v1:NextNumber(-1, 1)
    			local v4 = v1:NextNumber(-1, 1)

    				deviation = v12,
    				vec_deviation = Vector2.new(v3, v4).Unit * v22 * v1:NextNumber(0, 1) ^ p2.spread_factor
    			}
    }

    function t.update_health(p1, p2, p3) --[[ update_health | Line: 497 | Upvalues: FIRE_HURT_TYPE (copy) ]]
    	local tbl = {
    		{
    			hp = 10000,
    			blur = 7,
    			vignette = 0.2,
    			sat = 25,
    			rotMovement = 0.1
    		},
    		{
    			hp = 101,
    			blur = 0,
    			vignette = 1,
    			sat = 0,
    			rotMovement = 0.2
    		},
    		{
    			hp = 0,
    			blur = 5,
    			vignette = 0.4,
    			sat = -0.9,
    		}
    	}
    	for k, v in pairs(tbl) do
    		if p2 < v.hp and tbl[k + 1] then
    			local v1 = tbl[k + 1]
    			if v1.hp < p2 then
    				local v2 = (p2 - v.hp) / (v1.hp - v.hp)
    				if p2 < p1.health then
    					local v3 = math.lerp(v.rotMovement, v1.rotMovement, v2) * 400
    					local v4 = if math.random(0, 1) == 1 then -1 else 1
    					if p3 ~= FIRE_HURT_TYPE then
    						p1.adrenaline = p1.adrenaline + v3 * 0.015
    						p1.springs.camera:shove(Vector3.new(0, 0, v3 * 0.001) * v4)
    						p1.springs.camera:shove(Vector3.new(0, v3 * 0.0001, 0) * v4)
    						p1.springs.camera:shove((Vector3.new(v3 * 0.001, 0, 0)))
    				p1.health = p2

    local function clone_recentered_children(p1, p2) --[[ clone_recentered_children | Line: 3 ]]
    	local t = {}
    	for k, v in pairs(p1) do
    		local v1 = p2[v.name]
    		local t2 = {}
    		t2.cframe = if v1 then v1 * v.cframe else v.cframe
    		t2.name = v.name
    		t2.weight = v.weight
    		t[k] = t2
    return {
    	fix_track_keyframes = function(p1, p2) --[[ fix_track_keyframes | Line: 23 | Upvalues: clone_recentered_children (copy) ]]
    		if p1.sequence then
    			local children = p1.sequence.children
    			local v1 = table.create(#children)
    			for v2, v3 in children do
    				v1[v2] = {
    					children = clone_recentered_children(v3.children, p2),
    					name = v3.name,
    					time = v3.time
    				}
    			p1.sequence = {
    				children = v1,
    				name = p1.sequence.name
    			}
    	fix_pose_keyframes = function(p1, p2) --[[ fix_pose_keyframes | Line: 47 | Upvalues: clone_recentered_children (copy) ]]

    			p1.keyframe = {
    				children = clone_recentered_children(p1.keyframe.children, p2),
    				name = p1.keyframe.name,
    				time = p1.keyframe.time
    			}
    }

    		local v1 = string.split(p3, " ")

    		local v3 = v1[2]

    			local v7 = grenade_pins[v3]

    				local v14 = v10:GetAttribute("emit_count") and 1
    				for v15, v16 in v10:GetChildren() do
    					if v16:IsA("ParticleEmitter") then
    						v16:Emit(v14)
    			if v2 ~= "EVENT_SET_BULLET_TRANSPARENCY" or (v4 == nil or not p2.animations_properties.bullet_transparency_control) then
    			local Part1 = p1.weapon.viewmodel.receiver.bullet.Part1
    			if Part1 then
    				Part1.Transparency = v4
    				for v17, v18 in Part1:GetChildren() do
    					if v18:IsA("MeshPart") then
    						v18.Transparency = v4
    }

    local SHARED_STATE = require(ReplicatedStorage.module.shared_state).SHARED_STATE

    		p1:update_character(p12)
    		if p1.running and p1.is_prone then
    			p1:lie_down(false)
    		if p1.crouching and p1.running then
    			p1:crouch(false)
    		local pose = p1.simulation.animator.pose
    		local v1 = math.min(p12 * 10, 1)
    		local v2 = p1.default_properties.jump_power[pose]
    		local v3 = SharedPlayerLogic.get_walkspeed(pose, p1.aiming, p1.lean_side ~= "none", p1.char_data.collective_weight)
    		if not p1.landing_walkspeed_timer:expired() then
    			v3 = math.max(v3 * (1 - (p1.landing_walkspeed_timer.next_time - Timescale.get_time()) / p1.landing_walkspeed_timer.timeout), 1)
    		if p1.weapon.is_reloading and p1.running then
    			v3 = v3 * 0.85
    		local v6 = -p1.relative_char_velocity.Z / 20
    		local v7 = math.abs(p1.relative_char_velocity.X) / 50
    		local raycast_result = p1.simulation.raycast_result
    		if raycast_result.is_grounded then
    			v3 = v3 / (1 + ((raycast_result.normal or Vector3.new()) - Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)).Magnitude * 0.5)
    		if raycast_result.is_grounded ~= p1.grounded then
    				p1.last_jump_lookvector = workspace.Camera.CFrame.LookVector
    				p1.highest_jump_velocity = 0
    		if not raycast_result.is_grounded and p1.highest_jump_velocity < Velocity.Y then
    			p1.highest_jump_velocity = Velocity.Y
    		p1.last_grounded = p1.grounded
    		p1.grounded = raycast_result.is_grounded
    		if v6 < 0 then
    			v3 = v3 / (-v6 + 1)
    		local v10 = math.map(p1.stamina, 0, 40, 0.6, 1)
    		local v11 = v3 / (v7 + 1) * math.clamp(v10, 0, 1) * SHARED_STATE.plr_speed.value * Timescale.get_speed() * (p1.char_data.overrides.speed or 1)
    		if not p1.running then
    			p1.full_target_walkspeed = v11
    		p1.simulation.states.Walking.jump_height = (p1.aiming and v2.aiming or v2.standing) * (p1.char_data.overrides.jump_multiplier or 1)
    		local v18 = math.max(math.max(math.min(v11, (math.lerp(p1.simulation.states.Walking.target_speed, v11, (math.min(v1, 1))))), 1), 0)
    		local v20 = util.map_clamped(p1.char_data.collective_weight, 0, 7, SHARED_STATE.plr_movement_max_stiffness.value, SHARED_STATE.plr_movement_min_stiffness.value)
    		local v21 = Vector3.new(1.8, 3, 0.9)

    		if pose == "running" then
